In many aspects, it can‚Äôt even compare with chain hotels worth more than 300 yuan... First of all In terms of advantages, firstly, the view outside the window is first-class (but the windows are very dirty, so just try to watch it); secondly, the location is excellent, very close to the Drum Tower, Tianyi Square, etc. Third, I would like to praise the lady at the front desk who has straight bangs. Let‚Äôs talk about the shortcomings: First, the hygiene is worrying, the sticky trash can, and the sticky bedside alarm clock. I said that you should deliver the food together with the agreement. Then when it was finally delivered, I was not asked to sign it. I don‚Äôt think the request to have takeout delivered is excessive or troublesome. I have stayed in so many hotels, and every hotel can provide delivery service, and I have never been required to sign any agreement. Finally, the drinks and food in the small refrigerator are all charged (the key is that they are not valuable things, Harbin beer, Pepsi potato chips... Our room fee is nearly a thousand yuan, do we really need to worry about these things? ?)...The only free thing is Pepsi mineral water. Overall, I am very disappointed with Westin. I will not stay at Westin again when I come to Ningbo in the future.
